| `determ-wallet block-tx-root --block-json <file\|-> [--check] [--json]` | Offline recompute of the canonical `Block.tx_root` from a block JSON's `creator_tx_lists` — the exact validator accept gate (`compute_tx_root(creator_tx_lists)` vs stored `tx_root`; `src/node/validator.cpp`). `tx_root` is the commitment over the sorted-dedup UNION of the per-creator tx_hash lists (NOT a per-tx Merkle root, NOT the chained digest over tx signing_bytes): `{A,B}∪{B,C}={A,B,C}`, dedup collapses identical hashes, list/within-list order ignored, empty union = `SHA-256("")`. Mirrors `src/node/producer.cpp::compute_tx_root`. `--check` compares against the block's stored `tx_root` and exits 2 on mismatch (offline tamper-detection for a block from chain.json / CHAIN_RESPONSE / BLOCK gossip). `--json` emits `{recomputed_tx_root, stored_tx_root, leaf_count, match}`. Pure local SHA-256; no RPC/daemon/network; deterministic. Exit 0 success (or --check match), 1 args/parse/IO error, 2 --check mismatch. |
| `determ-wallet block-verify --block-json <file> [--committee <file>] [--block-digest <hex64>] [--json]` | Offline one-shot single-block verifier — composes three checks over an UNWRAPPED Block JSON (the `block-info --json` shape; a `{block:{...}}` envelope is rejected) into one PASS/FAIL with a monitor-friendly exit code, mirroring `determ-light audit`'s orchestration inside the wallet's chain-library-free TCB. **STRUCTURE**: block well-formedness (required `index`/`prev_hash`/`timestamp`/`creators[]`/`creator_tx_lists[]`/`tx_root`/`creator_block_sigs[]` with valid shapes; `creators[]` non-empty). **TX-ROOT**: recompute `compute_tx_root(creator_tx_lists)` == stored `tx_root` (delegates to `block-tx-root --check`; mirrors `src/node/producer.cpp::compute_tx_root` byte-for-byte — a TX-ROOT PASS is exactly the daemon's validator accept gate). **SIGS**: `ceil(2P/3)`-quorum Ed25519 committee-sig verification over the OPERATOR-SUPPLIED `--block-digest` (delegates to `committee-signature-verify`); attempted only when BOTH `--committee` and `--block-digest` are given, else **SKIP** — the wallet cannot recompute `compute_block_digest` (no chain-lib link), so the digest is operator-supplied (e.g. from `determ verify-block-sigs`). On STRUCTURE failure both downstream checks SKIP; a SKIP never masks a failure. Pure local crypto; no RPC/daemon. Default human output prints a per-check breakdown + a `BLOCK-VERIFY: PASS/FAIL (n passed, n failed, n skipped)` line; `--json` emits `{audit, passed, failed, skipped, checks:[{check, verdict, detail}]}` (delegated sub-command stdout+stderr captured to a sink). Soundness: `docs/proofs/OfflineBlockVerifySoundness.md` (BV-1 tx-root byte-equivalence to the daemon gate, BV-2 conditional-digest sig boundary, BV-3 composite/fail-closed). Exercised by `tools/test_wallet_block_verify.sh` (24 offline assertions). **Exit codes**: 0 all attempted checks pass, 2 a check FAILED, 1 args/parse/IO error. |
| `determ-wallet merkle-root --leaves <file> [--check <hex64>] [--json]` | Offline compute of the S-033 committed `state_root` from a FULL leaf set — the inverse of `state-proof-verify` (which checks ONE leaf's path against a root). Rebuilds the whole sorted-leaves balanced binary Merkle tree + the S-040 leaf-count wrap, byte-for-byte per `src/crypto/merkle.cpp::merkle_root`: leaves sorted by raw key bytes, `leaf=SHA-256(0x00‖u32_be(key_len)‖key‖value_hash)`, balanced tree with duplicate-last on odd rows, `inner=SHA-256(0x01‖L‖R)`, then `root=SHA-256(0x02‖u32_be(leaf_count)‖inner_root)` (the S-040 wrap binding leaf_count); an empty leaf set yields the all-zero root. Because determ-wallet does NOT link the chain library (TCB separation), the algorithm is reimplemented inline with OpenSSL SHA-256. `--leaves <file>` is a JSON array of `{value_hash:<64-hex>, key:<string> / key_hex:<hex>}` (key = UTF-8 bytes for ASCII namespaces a:/s:/r:/d:/k:/c:; key_hex = binary key for the composite i:/m:/p: keys; exactly one per entry). `--check <hex64>` compares the computed root to an expected committee-signed `state_root`, emitting VALID/INVALID and exiting 2 on mismatch — an offline full-state-root check against a signed header (the full-state dual of state-proof-verify's single-leaf membership check). `--json` emits `{root, leaf_count[, expected, match]}`. Pure local SHA-256; no RPC/daemon; deterministic. Soundness: `docs/proofs/MerkleRootRecomputeSoundness.md`. Exercised by `tools/test_wallet_merkle_root.sh` (16 offline assertions: Python-reference cross-check at 1/3/5/empty leaves, order-independence, key/key_hex equivalence, tamper sensitivity, --check exit codes, and a cross-command round-trip — a single-leaf root verifies VALID via `state-proof-verify`). **Exit codes**: 0 success (or --check match), 1 args/parse/IO error, 2 --check mismatch. |
| `determ-wallet merkle-proof --leaves <file> (--key <string> \| --key-hex <hex>) [--json]` | Offline generation of a Merkle inclusion proof for ONE leaf from a full leaf set — the proof GENERATOR completing the offline Merkle triad (`merkle-root` builds the committed `state_root`, `state-proof-verify` consumes a proof, `merkle-proof` generates one). Reproduces `src/crypto/merkle.cpp::merkle_proof` byte-for-byte (the wallet does NOT link the chain library — TCB separation): sorts the leaves by raw key bytes, locates the target key's SORTED index, then collects the sibling at each level (`idx^1`, duplicate-last on odd rows) reducing with `inner=SHA-256(0x01‖L‖R)`. Emits the EXACT `rpc_state_proof` reply shape `{key_bytes, value_hash, target_index, leaf_count, proof:[hex...], state_root}` (the `state_root` is the S-040-wrapped `merkle_root` over the same set, byte-identical to `merkle-root`), so the output round-trips directly: `merkle-proof ... --json > p.json; state-proof-verify --in p.json --root <state_root>` => VALID. Lets a developer/auditor construct proofs offline (fixture generation) or diff a generated proof against a daemon's served `state_proof` for the same `(namespace, key)`. `--leaves` is the `merkle-root` shape (`{value_hash, key/key_hex}`, unique keys); exactly one of `--key` (UTF-8) / `--key-hex` (binary composite i:/m:/p: keys) selects the target. Pure local SHA-256; no RPC/daemon; deterministic. Soundness: `docs/proofs/MerkleProofGenSoundness.md`. Exercised by `tools/test_wallet_merkle_proof.sh` (12 offline assertions — the load-bearing one being that EVERY leaf in a 5-leaf (odd, duplicate-last) and 4-leaf (even) set round-trips VALID through `state-proof-verify`, plus single-leaf empty proof, key/key_hex equivalence, tamper->INVALID, key-not-found). **Exit codes**: 0 success, 1 args/parse/IO error or target key not present. |
| `determ-wallet rpc-auth --method <m> [--params <json> \| --params-file <file>] --secret <hex> [--verify <hex> \| --request <file>] [--json]` | OFFLINE computor + verifier for the S-001 (v2.16) RPC HMAC-auth tag — the wallet-side dual of `RpcServer::verify_auth` / `rpc_call` (src/rpc/rpc.cpp). Derives the `auth` field a caller attaches to an RPC request, or verifies a claimed tag against a re-derivation, with no socket and no daemon. Scheme matches the daemon byte-for-byte: `key = hex_decode(secret)`; `canonical = method + "\|" + params.dump()` (compact, sorted keys); `auth = lowercase-hex(HMAC-SHA-256(key, canonical))`. Compute mode (default) prints the tag, canonical preimage, and a ready-to-send `{method,params,auth}` envelope; `--verify`/`--request` switch to constant-time verify. Secret never echoed (only its byte length). No RPC, no network, no subprocess. Exit 0 compute-OK / verify-MATCH, 1 args/parse error, 2 verify MISMATCH. |

## determ-light binary

A separate executable (built from `light/` source tree; CMake target `determ-light`) that implements a trust-minimized light-client wallet. Reads chain data via a daemon's RPC and locally verifies every response against (1) the pinned genesis hash, (2) committee-signed `state_root` Merkle inclusion proofs, (3) the prev_hash chain-of-hashes. Refuses to proceed on any verification failure. Signing uses the same canonical `signing_bytes` schema as `determ-wallet`'s `sign-anon-tx` — produced envelopes are byte-identical and round-trip through `submit_tx` on either binary.

The operator's daemon does NOT need HMAC RPC auth or rate limiting for `determ-light` to be safe: the light-client is the verifier and the daemon is the data-serving party. Even a malicious daemon cannot mislead an honest `determ-light` under the honest-majority-of-committee assumption.

| Command | Description |
|---|---|
| `determ-light verify-headers --in <file> [--genesis-hash <hex>] [--prev-hash <hex>]` | Verify the prev_hash chain in a `headers` RPC reply. `--genesis-hash` pins the index-0 anchor; `--prev-hash` pins a mid-chain start anchor. Each consecutive header's `prev_hash` must equal the prior's server-supplied `block_hash`. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_headers.sh`. **Exit codes**: 0 OK, 1 verification failure / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-block-sigs --header <file> --committee <file> [--bft]` | Verify K-of-K (or BFT-mode `ceil(2K/3)`) committee Ed25519 signatures on a single block header. Accepts either a bare-header JSON or a `{headers: [...]}` envelope. Committee file accepts a bare array or `{members: [...]}` (the format `determ validators --json` emits). Recomputes `compute_block_digest` byte-for-byte from header-only fields (no transactions / receipts needed). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_block_sigs.sh`. **Exit codes**: 0 quorum met + every sig verifies, 1 verification failure / malformed input. |
| `determ-light block-verify --block <file> --committee <file> [--bft] [--json]` | Self-contained OFFLINE single-block verifier — the light-client analogue of `determ-wallet block-verify`, but STRICTLY stronger: because determ-light links the chain digest code (`light_compute_block_digest`), it verifies the committee signatures against a digest it RECOMPUTES ITSELF, so NO operator-supplied `--block-digest` is needed (the wallet cannot recompute the digest — it does not link the chain library, hence its SIGS is conditional on a correct supplied digest; see `docs/proofs/OfflineBlockVerifySoundness.md` BV-2). Composes three checks over an (unwrapped or `{block:{...}}`-enveloped) Block JSON + committee file: **STRUCTURE** (required `index`/`prev_hash`/`timestamp`/`creators[]`/`creator_tx_lists[]`/`tx_root`/`creator_block_sigs[]` shapes; creators[] non-empty), **TX-ROOT** (recompute `compute_tx_root(creator_tx_lists)` — the sorted-dedup union SHA-256, mirroring `src/node/producer.cpp::compute_tx_root` byte-for-byte — == stored `tx_root`), and **SIGS** (K-of-K or `ceil(2K/3)` with `--bft` committee Ed25519 over the INTERNALLY-recomputed `block_digest`, via `verify_block_sigs`). Pure local crypto: no RPC, no daemon, no genesis anchor. The committee remains operator-supplied, so a PASS proves the block is signed by the SUPPLIED committee (derive the genuine committee trustlessly via `verify-chain` / `committee-at-height`) — a strictly smaller trust boundary than the wallet's (which needs both committee AND digest). Default human output prints a per-check breakdown + a `BLOCK-VERIFY: PASS/FAIL (n passed, n failed)` line; `--json` emits `{audit, passed, failed, checks:[{check, verdict, detail}]}`. On a cross-shard / F2-reconciled block the internally-recomputed digest omits the `compute_view_root` terms `compute_block_digest` binds for those (`light_compute_block_digest` scope), so SIGS FAIL-CLOSES there (false-negative, never a false PASS — verify those against a full node); non-cross-shard/non-F2 blocks keep the byte-identical v1 digest. Soundness: `docs/proofs/LightBlockVerifySoundness.md`. Exercised by `tools/test_light_block_verify.sh` (cluster: real-block PASS across all three checks + tampered-tx_root / tampered-sig / wrong-committee / malformed negatives). **Exit codes**: 0 all pass, 2 a check FAILED, 1 args/parse/IO error. |
| `determ-light committee-at-height --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --height <H> [--member <D>] [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless **committee-membership-at-height** reader — reports the committee-verified set of creators (the consensus committee) that produced block `H`, in selection order, each paired with its genesis-committee `ed_pub` + per-slot sign status (a sentinel-zero block-sig marks a BFT abstention). Distinct from `verify-block-sigs` (which checks sigs against a committee the OPERATOR supplies): `committee-at-height` **DERIVES** the committee trustlessly from the chain. Anchors genesis ONCE (fail-closed on hash mismatch), binds `header[H]` to block 0 via a prev_hash chain walk, and verifies header[H]'s K-of-K (MD) / `ceil(2K/3)`-of-`k_bft` (BFT) committee Ed25519 sigs over `light_compute_block_digest(H)` — which **BINDS `creators[]`** (`for (auto& c : b.creators) h.append(c)`), so the reported set is committee-attested, not merely daemon-asserted; a forged "header at H with a fabricated creator set" must both chain to genesis AND carry sigs over a digest committing to that set. Re-fetches `header[H]` and rebinds its `block_hash` to the attested value to catch a daemon serving a different header on re-fetch. Reuses the existing `verify_state_root_at` anchor (genesis pin + bounded prev_hash walk + committee-sig verification) — adds NO new crypto/Merkle/sig logic. With `--member <D>`, prints a sound **IN-COMMITTEE / NOT-IN-COMMITTEE** verdict plus the member's slot + sign status. Genesis (`H=0`) has no committee by construction and is rejected with a diagnostic; a sig failure or height-beyond-head fails closed (non-zero exit) — never a bare daemon-reported committee. **`--wait <seconds>`** (default 0 = unchanged) matters only when `H == head`: the S-042 successor binding needs block `H+1`, so a query at the exact head fails closed until the chain advances one block — `--wait` blocks for it; for any `H < head` the successor already exists and no wait is needed. `--json` emits `{height, block_hash, committee_size, sigs_verified, committee_verified, members:[{slot, domain, ed_pub, signed}], …}` (with `member` / `verdict` / `member_slot` / `member_signed` when `--member` is given). Exercised by `tools/test_light_committee_at_height.sh` (cluster-bound, single-node M=K=1: OK+creator-listed, `--member` IN/NOT-IN, no-false-positive, wrong-genesis fail-closed, H=0 rejected, height-beyond-head fail-closed, missing-flags usage error, `--json` shape). **Exit codes**: 0 committee reported OR (with `--member`) a sound IN-COMMITTEE/NOT-IN-COMMITTEE verdict, 3 UNVERIFIABLE membership (fail-closed reserve), 1 genesis pin mismatch / H=0 / committee-sig failure / height beyond head / unreachable daemon / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-state-proof --in <file> [--state-root <hex>]` | Verify a Merkle inclusion proof. Without `--state-root` the verify is self-consistent (siblings roll up to the proof's claimed root). With `--state-root` the proof's claimed root must match the operator-supplied anchor — defeats a daemon that fabricates a root to make its tampered proof verify against itself. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_state_proof.sh`. **Exit codes**: 0 OK, 1 verification failure / args error. |
| `determ-light fetch-headers --rpc-port <N> --from <I> --count <M> [--out <file>]` | Fetch headers `[I, I+M)` from `127.0.0.1:N` via the `headers` RPC. Without `--out` the envelope prints to stdout. **Exit codes**: 0 success, 1 RPC failure / args error. |
| `determ-light fetch-validators --rpc-port <N> [--out <file>]` | Fetch the current committee/creator set via the `validators` RPC and save the bare `{domain, ed_pub, active_from, registered_at, stake, region}` array (`node.cpp::rpc_validators`). Completes the **determ-light-only** offline verification workflow: `fetch-headers` + `fetch-validators` give an operator BOTH inputs for `verify-chain-file` / `committee-diff` using only the trust-minimized binary — no full `determ` node binary required. Unauthenticated read fetch (the committee is daemon-asserted; derive the genuine height-correct set trustlessly via `committee-at-height` when soundness matters). Without `--out` prints to stdout. Exercised by `tools/test_light_fetch_validators.sh` (cluster: byte-equals `determ validators --json`; end-to-end `fetch-headers`+`fetch-validators`→`verify-chain-file` PASS). **Exit codes**: 0 success, 1 RPC failure / args error. |
| `determ-light fetch-state-proof --rpc-port <N> --ns <NS> --key <K> [--out <file>]` | Fetch a state-proof from `127.0.0.1:N` via the `state_proof` RPC. NS is one of `a` (accounts) / `s` (stakes) / `r` (registrants) / `d` (DApps) / `b` (abort_records) / `k` (constants) / `c` (counters). **Exit codes**: 0 success, 1 RPC failure / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-chain --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> [--resume] [--persist [--state <path>]]` | Composite: (1) anchor genesis (compute local `compute_genesis_hash`, compare against daemon's block 0), (2) walk every header to the daemon's tip, (3) verify every block's K-of-K committee signatures against the genesis committee seed. Block 0 itself has no committee sigs (it's the deterministic GenesisConfig→Block seed) and is anchored via the genesis hash check; blocks 1..head are sig-verified. **`--persist`** caches the just-verified anchor (`{schema_version, genesis_hash, head_height, head_block_hash, head_state_root}`) to `--state <path>` (default `$DETERM_LIGHT_STATE`, else `~/.determ-light/state.json`) — written ONLY after the full committee-verify succeeds (never on a failed/unreachable verify, so the cache can never hold an unverified head). The persisted `genesis_hash` is the LOCAL recompute, so the pin a later run re-checks is the operator's own. **`--resume`** (LSP-6) re-pins the genesis against the cached anchor and verifies ONLY the suffix the daemon added above it — skipping the committee-signed prefix (each suffix block's K-of-K sig binds its `prev_hash`+`index`, so under SHA-256 collision resistance the first suffix block's `prev_hash == cached head_block_hash` transitively re-validates the skipped prefix). It falls back to a full verify when the anchor is absent / corrupt / for a different chain — never weaker than a full verify; a suffix that does not chain onto the anchor (a fork below it) is a HARD error (exit 1), never silently re-verified. **LSP-7 (head monotonicity):** with a VALID genesis-pinned anchor the cache is load-bearing evidence — a daemon whose head is BELOW the cached committee-verified height is REFUSED (a fork-free chain never regresses; stale/truncated state — clear with `state --clear` only for an intentional chain reset), and a daemon exactly AT it must present the cached anchor block itself (full verify + tip-vs-cache byte-compare; a block landing mid-check is handled by binding the anchor via the suffix walk). Pre-LSP-7 both cases silently full-verified and ACCEPTED the stale chain. Pair `--resume --persist` for the steady-state resume-then-advance loop. (A malicious daemon serving an index-0 suffix header to dodge the anchor/sig checks is rejected by the index-contiguity gate + the `verify_headers` anchored-page guard — see `LightStatePersistenceSoundness.md` LSP-6.) Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_chain.sh` + `tools/test_light_genesis_anchor.sh` (chain verify) + `tools/test_light_state.sh` (`--persist`/`--resume` arg contract + fail-closed-on-failure). **Exit codes**: 0 OK, 1 genesis pin mismatch (diagnostic cites "GENESIS HASH MISMATCH") / chain break / sig failure / resume fork-below-anchor. |
| `determ-light state (--show [--json] \| --clear \| --selftest \| --verify-anchor --genesis <file>) [--state <path>]` | **Offline persisted-anchor cache management** (no daemon contact) for the anchor written by `verify-chain --persist` (`light/persist.{hpp,cpp}`). `--show` loads + VALIDATES the cache and prints it incl. an `age` line from the file mtime (graceful "no anchor" on a missing file; **fails closed**, exit 1, on a corrupt one — never a false "no anchor"); `--show --json` emits a machine-readable `{present, path, schema_version, genesis_hash, head_height, head_block_hash, head_state_root, age_seconds}` (absent cache → `{"present": false, ...}` exit 0 — absence is data; corrupt cache stays fail-closed exit 1; `--json` is `--show`-only, rejected with any other mode) — the stable surface `tools/operator_anchor_audit.sh` consumes; `--clear` deletes it (graceful if already absent); `--selftest` runs the module's in-binary round-trip + fail-closed reject-path checks (save→load byte-equality, malformed JSON / bad `schema_version` / short-or-non-hex / missing-field all rejected) — the way save/load/validate is verified on a host where the cluster can't mint blocks; **`--verify-anchor --genesis <file>`** is the **offline genesis re-pin gate** (LSP-2): it recomputes `compute_genesis_hash` from the supplied genesis LOCALLY (no daemon) and reports **PASS** (exit 0) if the cached anchor's `genesis_hash` matches — i.e. the anchor is for THIS chain and a future `verify-chain --resume` could start from it — or **MISMATCH** (exit 2) if it is a stale/wrong-chain cache. This is exactly the gate the LSP-6 resume must run before trusting an anchor, landed + tested offline ahead of the daemon-bound resume itself. Path resolution: `--state <path>` › `$DETERM_LIGHT_STATE` › `~/.determ-light/state.json`. Trust model: the state file lives in the operator's TRUSTED LOCAL environment (`LightStatePersistenceSoundness.md` / `LightClientThreatModel.md` §6); a stale/wrong-chain cache is caught by this genesis pin + (on resume) forward committee re-verification, not by trusting the file. Exercised by `tools/test_light_state.sh` (27 offline assertions). **Exit codes**: 0 success / PASS / graceful-absence, 2 `--verify-anchor` MISMATCH, 1 corrupt-cache (fail-closed) / usage error. |
| `determ-light cross-check --genesis <file> (--rpc-port <N> \| --peer <host:port>) ×2+ [--json]` | **Multi-peer divergence detector** — closes the single-daemon limitation flagged across the light-client proof family (`LightClientCompositionMap.md` §6). Given ≥2 daemon endpoints — `--rpc-port <N>` (localhost) and/or `--peer <host:port>` (remote, cross-host via `RpcClient`'s getaddrinfo path, commit `9fed9ad`) — + a pinned `--genesis`, it INDEPENDENTLY committee-verifies each daemon's chain from genesis to head (reusing `anchor_genesis` + `verify_chain_to_head` — the same per-peer guarantee as `verify-chain`), then requires every pair of peers reporting the SAME height to agree on `(block_hash, state_root)`. Two genesis-anchored, committee-verified chains that DISAGREE at a shared height is a provable committee-signed fork / equivocation (a single honest canonical chain has exactly one block per height) → **DIVERGENCE** (a transferable equivocation witness feeding FA6). A peer merely BEHIND is benign **LAG** (reported, not compared). A peer that fails its own anchor/committee verify makes the whole check **UNVERIFIABLE** (fail-closed — you cannot cross-check against an unverifiable peer). Sound under {A1 committee-sig, A2 SHA-256} — no new assumption over per-peer `verify-chain`; adds eclipse/equivocation DETECTION across independent peers without weakening any single-peer guarantee. Does NOT detect an all-peers-collude set (needs ≥1 independent honest peer). Soundness: `docs/proofs/MultiPeerCrossCheckSoundness.md` (MPC-1..MPC-5). Exercised by `tools/test_light_cross_check.sh` (offline CLI/exit-code contract deterministic; live 2-daemon AGREE cluster-bound). **Exit codes**: 0 AGREE, 2 DIVERGENCE, 3 INCONCLUSIVE (no two peers share a height — retry), 1 UNVERIFIABLE / usage error. |
| `determ-light verify-chain-file --in <headers> (--committee <file> \| --committee-manifest <file>) [--genesis-hash <hex>] [--prev-hash <hex>] [--bft] [--json]` | Self-contained **OFFLINE whole-chain verifier** — the file-based dual of `verify-chain` (which fetches over RPC + anchors genesis via `compute_genesis_hash`). Given an EXPORTED headers file (the `fetch-headers` / `headers` RPC `{headers:[...], from}` shape) + committee material, verifies the whole exported segment with NO daemon: **CONTINUITY** (`verify_headers` prev_hash walk, optionally anchored at block 0 via `--genesis-hash` or mid-chain via `--prev-hash`) + **SIGS** (every non-genesis header's K-of-K — or `ceil(2K/3)` `--bft` — committee Ed25519 over its INTERNALLY-recomputed digest, via `verify_block_sigs`). ONLY index 0 (the sig-less genesis) is exempt; the skip keys on `index`, NOT on empty `creator_block_sigs` — because CONTINUITY walks the STORED `block_hash` linkage (it does not recompute sigs), an emptiness-based skip would let an edited headers file STRIP a real block's sigs to dodge verification, so a non-genesis header with stripped/empty sigs FAILS. A single `--committee` applies to every block (sound only across NO committee rotation); `--committee-manifest` — a JSON array `[{"from":F,"to":T,"committee":"path"}...]` mapping inclusive absolute-index ranges to committee files — verifies ACROSS rotation boundaries (per-range committee, lazy-loaded + cached; a block no range covers is a SIGS FAIL). Exactly one of `--committee` / `--committee-manifest` is required. No `compute_genesis_hash` on this path (the `--genesis-hash` anchor is matched against the file's own block-0 `block_hash`), so it is unaffected by the cross-platform genesis-hash gap. Cross-shard / F2 blocks fail-close in SIGS (F-LBV5). Soundness: `docs/proofs/LightVerifyChainFileSoundness.md`. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_chain_file.sh` (cluster: continuity+sigs PASS, `--json`, genesis-anchored PASS, manifest multi-range PASS + negatives: wrong genesis-hash / tampered prev_hash / tampered sig / STRIPPED non-genesis sigs / wrong-committee-per-range / uncovered-manifest-gap all FAIL exit 2). **Exit codes**: 0 all pass, 2 a check FAILED, 1 args/parse/IO error. |
| `determ-light committee-diff --a <file> --b <file> [--json]` | **Offline** diff of two committee files (the `determ validators --json` shape: a bare array, or `{members:[...]}`, of `{domain, ed_pub, region, stake}`) — the companion to `verify-chain-file --committee-manifest`. Reports which members were **added** / **removed** / **key-rotated** (same `domain`, new `ed_pub`) / **region-changed** / **stake-changed** / **unchanged** between snapshot A and B. The **SIGNING-SET** verdict keys on the `(domain, ed_pub)` pairs `verify_block_sigs` actually uses — region/stake-only deltas leave it `IDENTICAL` (they don't affect signature verification) — so an operator learns whether ONE `--committee` covers a headers segment spanning the two snapshots (`IDENTICAL`) or whether a rotation forces a `--committee-manifest` (`DIFFERS`). Order-independent; accepts both file shapes; case-insensitive `ed_pub`. Pure local JSON — no daemon, no crypto. Exercised by `tools/test_light_committee_diff.sh` (offline, 11 assertions: help, identical, reordered, `{members}`+uppercase, add/remove/rotate DIFFERS, region+stake-both-changed IDENTICAL, missing-domain parse error). **Exit codes**: 0 signing set IDENTICAL, 2 DIFFERS (rotation), 1 args/parse error. |
| `determ-light audit --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> [--json]` | One-shot composite trust-minimized node audit (monitor/cron health gate) — composes two whole-chain verifiers into a single PASS/FAIL with a monitor-friendly exit code, adding NO new verification logic. **CHAIN**: the `verify-chain` flow (`verify_chain_to_head`) — anchor genesis (local `compute_genesis_hash` vs daemon block 0; fail-closed on mismatch) + walk every header to head verifying prev_hash continuity + every block's K-of-K committee Ed25519 sigs; surfaces the head's `state_root`. **SUPPLY**: the `supply-trustless` flow (`cmd_supply_trustless`) — A1 unitary-supply conservation Merkle-verified against the SAME committee-signed head. SUPPLY runs only if CHAIN passes; on CHAIN failure it is reported **SKIP** (never PASS), so a SKIP can never mask a failed chain. Default human output prints a per-check breakdown then an `=== AUDIT SUMMARY ===` table + a final `AUDIT: PASS/FAIL (n passed, n failed, n skipped)` line; `--json` emits ONLY `{audit, passed, failed, skipped, head_state_root, checks:[{check, verdict, detail}]}` (the composed sub-commands' stdout AND stderr are captured to a sink so monitoring ingests clean JSON). Soundness: `docs/proofs/LightClientAuditComposition.md` (AC-1 composite soundness = CHAIN and SUPPLY, AC-2 no added trust surface, AC-3 fail-closed, AC-4 SKIP semantics, AC-E ≤ 2⁻⁹¹). Coverage is chain + supply only — per-account/dapp/receipt/merge/param membership each have their own `verify-*` command. Exercised by `tools/test_light_audit.sh` (cluster PASS path + fail-closed wrong-genesis negative). **Exit codes**: 0 all checks pass, 1 any check fails / CHAIN error / unreachable daemon / args error (a bad `--rpc-port` propagates to the top-level handler as exit 2). |
| `determ-light balance-trustless --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> [--json] [--resume [--state <path>]] [--wait <seconds>]` | Composite trustless balance read. Anchors genesis, walks chain to head, fetches state-proof for the account, cross-checks the daemon's cleartext `account` reply against the proof's `value_hash` (the daemon could lie about cleartext while serving an honest proof for a different account; the hash recomputation forces consistency). **`--resume`** reuses a cached committee-verified anchor (`verify-chain --persist`) — verifying only the suffix above it instead of re-walking from genesis on every read — via the shared `anchored_head` helper (the same LSP-6 resume path `verify-chain --resume` uses; falls back to a full verify when the cache is absent/corrupt/wrong-chain/not-ahead, never weaker). **`--wait <seconds>`** (opt-in; default 0 = unchanged) is the S-042 head-read usability path: when the anchor is the chain head — whose `state_root` has no committee-signed successor block yet, so a trustless read fails closed — it blocks up to N seconds polling for the next block to be produced, then binds the ALREADY-HELD proof (never re-fetched, which would race a state change); soundness is unchanged, only liveness at the live head. `--json` emits `{domain, balance, next_nonce, height, state_root, verified}` with `verified=true` on success. Exercised by `tools/test_light_balance_trustless.sh`. **Exit codes**: 0 verified balance returned, 1 verification failure (e.g., genesis mismatch, daemon tampered cleartext, stale state). |
| `determ-light nonce-trustless --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> [--json] [--resume [--state <path>]] [--wait <seconds>]` | Same composition as `balance-trustless` (incl. `--resume` via `anchored_head`) but the human-output line extracts `next_nonce` instead. `--json` output is identical (both fields present in either mode). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. Exercised by `tools/test_light_nonce_trustless.sh`. **Exit codes**: 0 verified nonce returned, 1 verification failure. |
| `determ-light stake-trustless --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> [--json] [--resume [--state <path>]] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trust-minimized **stake** read (R41 G3) — the `s:`-namespace analogue of `balance-trustless` (incl. `--resume` via `anchored_head`, and the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`). Anchors genesis, walks + committee-verifies the chain to head, fetches the `s:` (stakes) state-proof for `--domain`, Merkle-verifies it against the committee-signed `state_root`, and cross-checks the daemon's cleartext `stake_info` reply against the proof's `value_hash` (`value_hash = SHA256(u64_be(locked) ‖ u64_be(unlock_height))`, matching `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves`). Fails closed (non-zero exit, no output) on any verification mismatch — including a domain with no stake leaf (daemon `state_proof` returns `not_found`). `--json` emits `{domain, locked, unlock_height, height, state_root, verified}`. Reuses the `balance-trustless` verify/anchor helpers verbatim; only the namespace + decoded value fields differ. Soundness: `docs/proofs/StakeProofSoundness.md` (SP-1 committee-anchored `s:` leaf, SP-2 Merkle-proof soundness via A2, SP-3 S-040 leaf_count boundary). Exercised by `tools/test_light_stake_trustless.sh` (7 assertions, cluster-bound; light-vs-`determ stake_info` parity on `locked` + `unlock_height`). **Exit codes**: 0 verified stake returned, 1 verification failure / genesis mismatch / no stake leaf / unreachable daemon. |
| `determ-light verify-abort-record --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> [--json] [--resume [--state <path>]] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trust-minimized **abort-record** read — the `b:`-namespace (S-032 `abort_records`) analogue of `stake-trustless`, completing the determ-light state-namespace reader coverage (`b:` was previously unreadable). Anchors genesis, walks + committee-verifies the chain to head, fetches the `b:` state-proof for `--domain` (node id), Merkle-verifies it against the committee-bound `state_root` (via `committee_bound_state_root`, the S-042 successor binding), and cross-checks the daemon's `abort_records` RPC cleartext against the proof's `value_hash` (`value_hash = SHA256(u64_be(count) ‖ u64_be(last_block))`, matching `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves`), so a lying daemon can neither inflate nor hide a node's FA5 Phase-1 abort count. **RECORDED** reports the committee-verified `(count, last_block)`; **NOT-RECORDED** (daemon `state_proof` `not_found`) is a daemon-asserted negative — sound only under the single-daemon (H-neg) honesty premise (`docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` NV-2/NV-3), tagged `"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"` in `--json`. A `b:` state-proof present while the `abort_records` cleartext omits the node → **INCONSISTENT** fail-closed (the daemon is lying about one or the other). The trust-minimized complement to `tools/operator_slashing_ledger.sh`. `--json` emits `{domain, verdict, count, last_block, height, state_root, verified}`. Reuses the `stake-trustless` verify/anchor/bind helpers; only the namespace + decoded fields differ. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_abort_record.sh` (offline contract: help/usage/bad-`--wait`/no-daemon fail-closed; live RECORDED/NOT-RECORDED/tamper legs are CI/WSL2). Soundness: `docs/proofs/AbortRecordProofSoundness.md` (AB-1 key-bind + committee anchor, AB-2 cleartext hash-bind, AB-3 daemon-asserted negative, AB-4 Phase-1-only boundary). **Exit codes**: 0 verified verdict (RECORDED / NOT-RECORDED — the verdict is in the output), 1 verification failure (tamper / root mismatch / INCONSISTENT) / genesis mismatch / unreachable daemon / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-constant --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --name <NAME> {--value <U64> \| --value-hex <64-hex>} [--json] [--resume [--state <path>]] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trust-minimized **chain-constant** read for the `k:` (genesis-pinned constants) namespace. `verify-param-value` already reads the 12 u64 `k:` constants; this command's delta is **`shard_salt` coverage** (the 32-byte leaf no prior reader could assert), a **closed compiled-in name whitelist** (unknown names rejected before any RPC), `--resume` support, and a **MISMATCH-exit-2 contract** (`verify-param-value` exits 0 on MISMATCH — consumers gating on exit codes get a sound non-zero signal here). CONFIRM-shaped (`k:` has no cleartext RPC): the OPERATOR asserts `(name, value)` and the reader proves the assertion against the committee-attested `k:` leaf — key-bound (`proof.key_bytes == "k:"+name`, the F-6 closure) and Merkle-bound to the committee-signed `state_root` via `committee_bound_state_root` (S-042). **BOTH verdicts are cryptographic** (no daemon-asserted negative exists here, because every `k:` leaf is unconditionally committed by `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves`): **CONFIRMED** (exit 0) = the committee attests exactly `SHA256(u64_be(value))` (or `SHA256(salt)` for `shard_salt`); **MISMATCH** (exit 2) = the committee-bound leaf commits a DIFFERENT value than asserted (sound under A2 — the chain does not run this parameter value); `not_found` → **UNVERIFIABLE** (exit 3 — a legacy/pre-S-033 or lying daemon, never a negative verdict). The 12 u64 constants (`block_subsidy`, `subsidy_pool_initial`, `subsidy_mode`, `lottery_jackpot_multiplier`, `min_stake`, `suspension_slash`, `unstake_delay`, `merge_threshold_blocks`, `revert_threshold_blocks`, `merge_grace_blocks`, `shard_count`, `my_shard_id`) take `--value <u64>`; `shard_salt` (a 32-byte leaf) takes `--value-hex <64-hex>`; unknown names are rejected listing the canonical set (the NV-5a canonical-key discipline — the daemon never picks the key). Use case: audit that a daemon's chain runs the governance parameters the operator expects without trusting its config or logs. `--json` emits `{name, verdict, asserted_value[_hex], height, state_root, verified}`. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_constant.sh` (offline contract: help / canonical-name gate / value-form gates / bad-`--wait` / no-daemon fail-fast; live CONFIRMED / MISMATCH-exit-2 / UNVERIFIABLE / key-bind legs are CI/WSL2). **Exit codes**: 0 CONFIRMED, 2 MISMATCH (sound — committee attests a different value), 3 UNVERIFIABLE (daemon refused `k:`), 1 genesis mismatch / unknown name / value-form error / unreachable daemon / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-unstake-eligibility --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Committee-anchored S-017 unstake-eligibility verdict: composes `stake-trustless` (anchor genesis + committee-verify the header chain to head + Merkle-verify the `s:` leaf + hash-bind the daemon's `stake_info` cleartext) then re-runs the validator's `(H+1) >= unlock_height` gate over the committee-attested unlock_height (H = the committee-verified head height). **`--wait <seconds>`** (default 0 = unchanged) forwards to the embedded `stake-trustless` read, which anchors at the head and so hits the same S-042 head-read fail-closed as the standalone readers: it blocks up to N seconds for the head's successor block, then binds the already-held proof. Without it the verdict is **UNVERIFIABLE** at the live head unless a block happens to land mid-read. Note the verdict is head-relative, so waiting advances the verified head H by one block (correct — the verdict is always "as of the committee-verified head"). Both inputs to the predicate (head H via the verified header chain, unlock_height via the hash-bound `s:` leaf) are committee-anchored, so an ELIGIBLE / LOCKED / BONDED verdict cannot be faked by a lying daemon. Distinct from `stake-trustless` (which only reports the raw `(locked, unlock_height)` pair without the height-relative verdict). Verdicts: **ELIGIBLE** / **LOCKED** (+`blocks_remaining`) / **BONDED** (`unlock_height == UINT64_MAX` — no DEREGISTER scheduled) / **NO-STAKE** (`locked == 0` or no `s:` leaf) — all exit 0; tamper / mismatch / daemon refusal → **UNVERIFIABLE** (exit 3), never a false ELIGIBLE. **NO-STAKE has two footings** (`docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` F-2): a present `s:` leaf with `locked == 0` is a committee-anchored positive proof of a zero stake (`"negative_footing": "cryptographic"` in `--json`), while a `state_proof not_found` absence is a **daemon-asserted negative** — sound only under the single-daemon (H-neg) honesty premise, NV-2/NV-3 (`"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"`). Only the literal `not_found` marker classifies as absence; any other state-proof refusal is UNVERIFIABLE (the former broader matcher mapped every RPC error to NO-STAKE — NegativeVerdictSoundness.md F-5, fixed). Predicate mirrors `src/node/validator.cpp BlockValidator::check_tx` (`b.index < stake_unlock_height` rejects) and `src/node/node.cpp rpc_stake_info`. `--json` emits the verdict + committee-attested fields. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_unstake_eligibility.sh` (10 assertions, SKIP-clean when `DETERM_LIGHT` unset). **Exit codes**: 0 sound verdict (ELIGIBLE / LOCKED / BONDED / NO-STAKE — the verdict is in the output), 3 UNVERIFIABLE (fail-closed on tamper / mismatch / refusal), 1 genesis mismatch / missing args / unreachable daemon. |
| `determ-light supply-trustless --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> [--json] [--resume [--state <path>]] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless A1 unitary-supply conservation read. Anchors genesis, committee-verifies the header chain to head (or `--resume` only the suffix above a cached anchor, via the shared `anchored_head` helper; opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`), then fetches a `c:`-namespace state-proof for each of the five supply counters (`genesis_total`, `accumulated_subsidy`, `accumulated_inbound`, `accumulated_slashed`, `accumulated_outbound`), Merkle-verifies each against the SAME committee-signed `state_root` (rejecting the split-root attack), and hash-binds each counter's `chain_summary` cleartext via `SHA256(u64_be(v)) == proof.value_hash`. Recomputes the closed-form A1 identity (`genesis_total + subsidy + inbound - slashed - outbound`) from the committed values and compares it to the daemon's claimed `total_supply`. Unlike the single-leaf `a:`/`s:` reads this is a CROSS-LEAF invariant recheckable from committed values alone; it does NOT enumerate every account, so `live_total_supply` is cross-checked, not independently re-derived (the S-040 `leaf_count` boundary). Exercised by `tools/test_light_supply_trustless.sh`. **Exit codes**: 0 CONSERVED, 2 VIOLATED, 3 UNVERIFIABLE (tamper / split-root / daemon refusal — never a false CONSERVED), 1 transport / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-account --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> {--pubkey <64-hex> \| --address <0x...>} [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Derive an anon-account's canonical address locally (make_anon_address / S-028 normalization) and prove EXISTS / NOT-CREATED against the committee-verified `a:` namespace, exercising the account auto-creation-on-first-credit lifecycle. EXISTS reports the committee-anchored balance + next_nonce (hash-bound to the daemon `account` cleartext); NOT-CREATED (state_proof `not_found`) is a **daemon-asserted negative** — sound only under the single-daemon (H-neg) honesty premise (`docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` NV-2/NV-3), stronger than the bare fabricated zero the `account` RPC returns for unknown addresses but NOT a cryptographic absence proof; tagged `"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"` in `--json` (F-2). EXISTS/NOT-CREATED -> exit 0; tamper/mismatch/refusal -> UNVERIFIABLE (exit 3). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. |
| `determ-light sign-tx --keyfile <path> --type {TRANSFER\|STAKE\|UNSTAKE} --to <addr> --amount N --fee N --nonce N [--out <file>]` | Offline TRANSFER / STAKE / UNSTAKE signing. Loads the keyfile (canonical `{address, privkey_hex}` shape OR alternate `{ed_priv_hex, ed_pub_hex, anon_address}`), derives the Ed25519 pubkey via OpenSSL, cross-checks against the address (S-028 lowercase canonical), then signs over the canonical `signing_bytes` schema. Emits both `sig` (chain wire format) and `signature` (sign-anon-tx wire format) so the envelope is interchangeable with `determ-wallet` outputs. The envelope round-trips through `submit_tx` byte-identical. Exercised by `tools/test_light_sign_tx.sh` (which cross-verifies the produced envelope through `determ-wallet validate-tx` for byte-for-byte cross-binary parity). **Exit codes**: 0 success, 1 args / validation failure (missing flags, anon-address case violation, amount=0, keyfile-address mismatch). |
| `determ-light submit-tx --rpc-port <N> --tx-json <file>` | Submit a pre-signed tx envelope via the daemon's `submit_tx` RPC. The light-client wraps the envelope as `{"tx": <signed-json>}` matching `rpc.cpp` params shape. **Exit codes**: 0 submitted, 1 RPC error (typically "stale nonce" / "signature verification failed" / "S-018" missing-field diagnostics from the chain). |
| `determ-light verify-and-submit --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --keyfile <path> --to <addr> --amount N --fee N [--out <file>] [--resume [--state <path>]] [--wait <seconds>]` | End-to-end composite: trustless-fetch the sender's nonce, sign locally with that verified nonce, submit via `submit_tx`. **`--resume`** reuses a cached committee-verified anchor (`verify-chain --persist`) for the embedded nonce read via the shared `anchored_head` helper — the same resume path as the standalone reads; falls back to a full verify when the cache is unusable. **`--wait <seconds>`** (default 0 = unchanged) is forwarded to the embedded nonce read, which anchors at the head and so hits the same S-042 head-read fail-closed as the standalone readers: it blocks up to N seconds for the head's successor block, then binds the already-held proof (sound — never re-fetches). Without it, this flow only succeeds if a block happens to land between the proof fetch and the successor check. Output JSON has `verified_at_height`, `verified_nonce`, `verified_balance`, `state_root`, `submitted_tx_hash`, `submit_reply`. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_and_submit.sh` end-to-end (cluster boot → verify-and-submit → second balance-trustless confirming the transfer landed). **Exit codes**: 0 submitted, 1 verification or submit failure. |
| `determ-light watch-head --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> [--interval <S>] [--count <N>]` | Periodic trust-minimized head + committee-sig monitor (R39+1 A3). Anchors genesis ONCE at startup (fail-closed on hash mismatch — diagnostic mentions "GENESIS HASH MISMATCH" with exit non-zero), then polls the daemon's head every `--interval` seconds (default 1 s). Each tick re-fetches the head header via the `headers` RPC, re-runs `verify_block_sigs` against the genesis-seeded committee, and prints one structured line: `TICK <i>: height=<H> head_hash=<short> state_root=<short> committee_size=<K> sigs_valid=<yes\|no>`. Exits cleanly on SIGINT (interruptible 1-sec sleep granularity) or after `--count N` ticks (default unlimited). Transient RPC / sig-verify failure prints a WARN line and continues polling — the operator wants visibility, not silent exits. The light-client never trusts the daemon: every tick re-verifies the K-of-K committee signatures from scratch against the genesis-anchored committee, so a daemon serving a tampered head is caught at the first tick. Use cases: low-cost continuous monitoring from a SOC-style dashboard (operator runs a `watch-head` per validator and alerts on `sigs_valid=no`), chain-stall detection by observing `height` not advancing, light-client-grade post-deploy smoke ("the daemon is producing well-signed blocks against our pinned genesis"). Exercised by `tools/test_light_watch_head.sh` (4 assertions across boot-and-2-tick / wrong-genesis-startup / structured-line-shape / single-tick scenarios). **Exit codes**: 0 SIGINT-clean shutdown OR `--count` exhausted (regardless of per-tick sigs_valid status — the per-tick result is in the line output), 1 startup failure (genesis pin mismatch, unreachable daemon, malformed `--genesis` file, bad args). |
| `determ-light export-headers --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --from <H1> --count <M> --out <file> [--include-committee-sigs]` | Capture a verifiable header archive for off-chain audit (R39+2 B3) — composes FETCH+VERIFY+WRITE into a single self-contained artifact an auditor can re-verify offline at any later date without re-contacting the daemon (e.g. an immutable record of the chain across one fiscal quarter). Anchors genesis ONCE (fail-closed on hash mismatch — diagnostic mentions "GENESIS HASH MISMATCH"), fetches headers `[H1, H1+M)` via the `headers` RPC, verifies each header's K-of-K (or BFT-mode `ceil(2K/3)`) committee Ed25519 signatures against the genesis-seeded committee, then writes the archive JSON `{exported_at_height, from, count, genesis_hash, headers: [{index, header_json, verified_committee_sigs}, …]}` to `--out`. `--include-committee-sigs` embeds the per-block committee-signature material so the archive re-verifies fully standalone (larger artifact); without it the archive carries the `verified_committee_sigs=true` assertion recorded at export time (smaller). The exported file round-trips through `determ-light verify-headers --in <archive>` for the prev_hash chain-of-hashes re-check. Exercised by `tools/test_light_export_headers.sh` (boots a 3-node cluster, advances ~10 blocks, asserts archive shape, genesis anchor, the size delta between sig-include modes, out-of-range rejection, and the re-verification round-trip). **Exit codes**: 0 archive written + every header verified, 1 genesis pin mismatch / sig-verify failure / out-of-range range / RPC failure / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-archive --in <archive> --genesis <file> [--require-sigs]` | **OFFLINE** re-verification of an `export-headers` archive (R39+3 C3) — closes the audit loop with `export-headers`: that command verified the archive at CAPTURE time against a live daemon; `verify-archive` re-verifies it at AUDIT time (months later) against **nothing but the genesis file and the archive bytes**. Opens NO RPC client and touches NO network — pure local cryptographic re-check. Flow is LOAD → ANCHOR → CHAIN-CHECK → SIG-CHECK: (1) parse the archive JSON `{exported_at_height, from, count, genesis_hash, headers: [...]}`; (2) anchor — assert `compute_genesis_hash(genesis) == archive.genesis_hash` so an archive claiming a different chain is refused (the genesis file is the sole trust anchor); (3) re-walk the prev_hash chain via `verify_headers` (each header's `prev_hash` equals the prior's `block_hash`); (4) re-verify each non-genesis header's K-of-K (or BFT-mode `ceil(2K/3)`) committee Ed25519 signatures via `verify_block_sigs` against the genesis-seeded committee. Reuses the existing `light/` primitives (`load_genesis` / `compute_genesis_hash` / `build_genesis_committee` / `verify_headers` / `verify_block_sigs`) — re-implements no primitive. `--require-sigs` makes committee-sig re-verification **mandatory**: an archive exported WITHOUT `--include-committee-sigs` (creator_block_sigs stripped) fails with a clear "archive has no committee sigs" diagnostic; without `--require-sigs`, sigs are re-verified opportunistically (checked if retained, skipped if stripped — the genesis anchor + prev_hash chain still run). On success prints `OK: N headers verified (genesis anchored, prev_hash chain intact, K committee-sig sets valid)`. Cross-references `docs/proofs/LightClientArchiveSoundness.md` (AR-1..AR-4: AR-3 records that the archive's `exported_at_height` is an unverified exporter claim, so range-completeness is the auditor's obligation; AR-4 records that export + verify both use the static genesis committee K_0). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_archive.sh` (17 assertions covering offline round-trip via `export-headers` → `verify-archive`, genesis-mismatch rejection, prev_hash-chain-break rejection, committee-sig-tamper rejection, `--require-sigs` on a sigs-stripped archive, and bad-index diagnostics). **Exit codes**: 0 archive verified, 1 file/parse error / schema mismatch / genesis-hash mismatch / prev_hash chain break / committee-sig failure / `--require-sigs` on a sigs-stripped archive / args error. |
| `determ-light account-history --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> --from <H1> --to <H2> [--step <S>] [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless verified balance/nonce **trajectory** over a height range (D3 R40) — a verified sequence of `(height, balance, nonce)` rows for account `D` sampled across `[H1, H2]` at stride `--step` (default 1). Anchors genesis ONCE at startup (fail-closed on hash mismatch — diagnostic mentions "GENESIS HASH MISMATCH"), then for each sampled height `h`: fetches `header[h]`, verifies its committee Ed25519 signatures (MD K-of-K with BFT `ceil(2K/3)` fallback) + the `prev_hash` linkage back to the genesis-anchored chain, and records the committee-verified `state_root` at `h`. **Head-only-state-proof caveat (important):** the daemon's `state_proof` / `account` RPCs serve the CURRENT head only — so each sampled height's `state_root` is committee-verified (via header verification), but balance/nonce are Merkle-verified against a `state_proof` only at HEAD (a single `read_account_trustless` Merkle-read at the verified head). Each row is annotated with `balance_proven_at_height` (the height at which balance/nonce were Merkle-proven — the head) and `balance_merkle_verified` (true ONLY when the sampled height IS the head; false for historical rows, which carry the head-anchored values). The implementation is height-generic and auto-upgrades to per-height Merkle verification if the daemon's `state_proof` RPC gains a height parameter. Surfaces a nonce-monotonicity cross-check across rows (a violation is flagged as a daemon/chain inconsistency — see `docs/proofs/AccountHistorySoundness.md` AH-3: monotonicity is necessary-not-sufficient, a defense-in-depth tripwire, NOT the soundness guarantee). `--json` emits `{domain, from, to, step, head_height, rows: [{height, balance, next_nonce, state_root, balance_merkle_verified, balance_proven_at_height}, …]}`. Soundness proof: `docs/proofs/AccountHistorySoundness.md` (AH-1 per-point soundness via committee-sig + state-proof, AH-2 independent per-row anchoring, AH-3 nonce-monotonicity caveat, AH-4 sampling-gap honesty — the trajectory proves the values AT the sampled heights only, not between samples). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless` (the head-anchored Merkle read is the one affected). Exercised by `tools/test_light_account_history.sh` (cluster-bound). **Exit codes**: 0 trajectory emitted (every sampled row verified through its committee-signed header), 1 genesis pin mismatch / committee-sig failure at some sampled height / unreachable daemon / out-of-range / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-tx-inclusion --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --tx-hash <hex> --height <B> [--json]` | Trustless transaction-inclusion verifier (E3 R40) — a per-invocation INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED / UNVERIFIABLE verdict on whether transaction `H` (`--tx-hash`) is in the committee-signed block at height `B` (`--height`), without trusting the daemon. Anchors genesis ONCE (fail-closed on hash mismatch — "GENESIS HASH MISMATCH"), establishes header trust for block `B` (prev_hash continuity + K-of-K committee Ed25519 sigs), then **recomputes the union `tx_root` from the served block body and gates on byte-equality with the committee-signed `tx_root`** before scanning for `H`. **STRONG regime**: `tx_root` is part of the committee-signed block digest (`compute_block_digest` binds it, mirrored light-side in `light_compute_block_digest`), so a daemon cannot forge inclusion/non-inclusion — a tampered or omitted-tx body changes the recomputed root and yields UNVERIFIABLE (never a false verdict), and a daemon serving a body whose `tx_root` mismatches the committee-signed value is rejected. Because `tx_root` and `state_root` are independent block fields, this verifier has **no S-033/S-038 deployment prerequisite** (works on pre-S-033 blocks, unlike the balance/nonce reads). At `--height 0` the genesis block carries no committee sigs and an empty tx set, so it is anchored by genesis-hash match and reports **NOT-INCLUDED** for any `H`. `--json` emits `{included, verdict, height, …}`; a NOT-INCLUDED verdict additionally carries `"negative_footing": "cryptographic"` (F-2 of `docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` — this block-body negative is a SOUND absence proof, NV-1, so a consumer MAY treat it as authoritative; contrast the state-proof verifiers' `daemon_asserted`). Soundness proof: `docs/proofs/TxInclusionProofSoundness.md` (TI-1 sound positive inclusion, TI-2 sound non-inclusion, TI-3 tampered-body detection, TI-4 degradation-honesty — the regime Determ is NOT in; per-invocation bound `(B+K+2)·2⁻¹²⁸`). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_tx_inclusion.sh` (cluster-bound; real tx → INCLUDED, absent tx → NOT-INCLUDED, tampered/omitted body → UNVERIFIABLE, creator-not-in-seed → UNVERIFIABLE). **Exit codes**: 0 verdict emitted (INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED / UNVERIFIABLE — the verdict is in the output), 1 genesis pin mismatch / unreachable daemon / missing block `B` / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-receipt-inclusion --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --src-shard <S> --tx-hash <hex> [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless **cross-shard receipt-membership** verifier (R41 I3) — an INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED / UNVERIFIABLE verdict on whether the inbound receipt `(src_shard, tx_hash)` is in the committee-verified `i:` (applied_inbound_receipts) namespace, the `i:`-namespace analogue of `verify-tx-inclusion`. Anchors genesis, committee-verifies the chain to head, computes the canonical receipt key (`"i:" + u64_be(src_shard) + tx_hash`), fetches the `i:` state-proof, and Merkle-verifies it against the committee-signed `state_root` — binding the proof to *this* receipt via `key_bytes == local key` AND `value_hash == SHA256(0x01)` (the presence marker; all receipt identity lives in the Merkle KEY, not a value decode). Receipts are append-only once applied, so there is no per-block race. Fails closed: INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED → exit 0, UNVERIFIABLE → exit 3, errors → 1. The daemon's `state_proof` RPC **serves** the composite-key `i:` namespace (R-ext sourcing): the caller hex-encodes the binary key body (`u64_be(src_shard) ‖ tx_hash`) — raw bytes can't ride a JSON string, since a SHA-256 `tx_hash` breaks UTF-8 `dump()` — and the daemon hex-decodes it, length-checks it, and prepends `i:` to rebuild the canonical leaf key (`src/node/node.cpp` rpc_state_proof; `m:`/`p:` served identically). So an applied receipt yields a **real INCLUDED** (the `i:` state-proof Merkle-verified against the committee-signed `state_root`) and a never-applied key yields **NOT-INCLUDED** (`not_found`, a daemon-asserted negative — (H-neg)); UNVERIFIABLE arises only against a legacy daemon that cannot serve `i:`, or on any tamper/inconsistency (fail-closed — never a false INCLUDED). Soundness: `docs/proofs/ReceiptInclusionProofSoundness.md` (RI-1..RI-5; RI-3 one-sided-verifier honesty — a withheld leaf stays UNVERIFIABLE, never an authoritative NOT-APPLIED). A NOT-INCLUDED verdict carries `"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"` (F-2 of `docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` — the state-proof negative is sound only under the single-daemon (H-neg) honesty premise, NV-2/NV-3, so a consumer MUST treat it as "no proof obtained" per NV-6 clause 3, NOT as authoritative absence). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_receipt_inclusion.sh` (2-shard cross-shard flow: transfers A→B, reads the applied receipt out of shard-1 block bodies, then asserts a **real INCLUDED** for it + NOT-INCLUDED for a random hash + wrong-genesis + malformed-hash + missing-flag rejection + `--json` shape). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. **Exit codes**: 0 INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED, 3 UNVERIFIABLE, 1 genesis mismatch / unreachable daemon / args error. |
| `determ-light verify-merge-state --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --shard-id <S> --partner-id <P> --refugee-region <R> [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless **under-quorum-merge membership** verifier — an INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED / UNVERIFIABLE verdict on whether shard `S` is currently merged into partner `P` with refugee region `R`, i.e. whether the *exact* record `(partner_id=P, refugee_region=R)` is a member of the committee-verified `m:` (merge_state) namespace. The `m:`-namespace sibling of `verify-receipt-inclusion` (`i:`), reusing the same composite-key `state_proof` path the daemon now serves (`src/node/node.cpp` rpc_state_proof — caller hex-encodes the binary key body, daemon hex-decodes, length-checks `u32_be(shard_id)` = 4 bytes, and prepends `m:` to rebuild the canonical leaf key). Anchors genesis, committee-verifies the chain to head, computes the canonical merge key (`"m:" + u32_be(shard_id)`), fetches the `m:` state-proof, and Merkle-verifies it against the committee-signed `state_root` — binding the proof to *this* record via `key_bytes == local key` AND `value_hash == SHA256(u64_be(partner_id) ‖ u64_be(region_len) ‖ region)` (matching `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves`). **The value_hash binding is load-bearing** (unlike `i:`, whose value is the constant presence marker `SHA256(0x01)`): a `m:` leaf carries DATA, so a daemon could serve a valid Merkle proof for shard `S` that encodes a *different* partner/region — recomputing the hash from the caller-asserted `(partner_id, refugee_region)` forces the proof to match exactly that record, so a daemon lie about either field is detected, not propagated. **merge_state is mutable**: INCLUDED means "merged into `P` with region `R` AS OF the committee-verified head" (always reported with the head height it was proven at), and a later MERGE_END revert flips the same query to NOT-INCLUDED. Fails closed: INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED → exit 0 (NOT-INCLUDED is a daemon-asserted negative from a daemon `not_found` — (H-neg)), UNVERIFIABLE → exit 3 (legacy daemon that cannot serve `m:`, or any tamper/key-or-value mismatch — never a false INCLUDED), errors → 1. Input is validated before any verdict: `--shard-id`/`--partner-id` must fit u32, `--refugee-region` ≤ 32 bytes (the MERGE_EVENT wire ceiling). Soundness: `docs/proofs/MergeStateSoundness.md` (MS-3 `m:` leaf injectivity + state-root sensitivity under A2; MS-1 apply-determinism; MS-4 snapshot round-trip identity). A NOT-INCLUDED verdict carries `"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"` (F-2 of `docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` — sound only under the (H-neg) honesty premise NV-2/NV-3; NV-6 clause 3: not authoritative absence). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_merge_state.sh` (cluster-bound, EXTENDED 2-shard topology; SKIP-clean headline INCLUDED when an active merge exists, plus always-run random-shard → NOT-INCLUDED, wrong-genesis, out-of-range-shard-id, and missing-flag rejection assertions). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. **Exit codes**: 0 INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED, 3 UNVERIFIABLE, 1 genesis mismatch / out-of-range or missing args / unreachable daemon. |
| `determ-light verify-param-change --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --effective-height <H> --idx <I> --name <NAME> [--value-hex <HEX>] [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless **staged-governance-parameter membership** verifier — an INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED / UNVERIFIABLE verdict on whether the staged param change at index `I` within effective-height bucket `H`, named `NAME` with value `HEX`, is currently a member of the committee-verified `p:` (pending_param_changes) namespace, i.e. STILL STAGED (not yet activated). The `p:`-namespace sibling of `verify-merge-state` (`m:`) and `verify-receipt-inclusion` (`i:`), reusing the same composite-key `state_proof` path the daemon serves (`src/node/node.cpp` rpc_state_proof — caller hex-encodes the binary key body, daemon hex-decodes, length-checks `u64_be(eff_height) ‖ u32_be(idx)` = 12 bytes, and prepends `p:` to rebuild the canonical leaf key). Anchors genesis, committee-verifies the chain to head, computes the canonical key (`"p:" + u64_be(effective_height) + u32_be(idx)`), fetches the `p:` state-proof, and Merkle-verifies it against the committee-signed `state_root` — binding the proof to *this* change via `key_bytes == local key` AND `value_hash == SHA256(u64_be(name_len) ‖ name ‖ u64_be(value_len) ‖ value)` (matching `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves`; value bytes appended only when non-empty). **The value_hash binding is load-bearing** (like `m:`, unlike `i:`'s constant presence marker): a `p:` leaf carries DATA, so a daemon could serve a valid Merkle proof for slot `(H, I)` that encodes a *different* parameter name/value — recomputing the hash from the caller-asserted `(name, value_hex)` forces the proof to match exactly that staged change, so a daemon lie about either field is detected, not propagated. **pending_param_changes is mutable**: INCLUDED means "this exact change is STILL STAGED AS OF the committee-verified head" (reported with the head height it was proven at), and once the chain advances past `H` (`activate_pending_params` consumes the bucket) the same query flips to NOT-INCLUDED. Discover the `(effective_height, name, value_hex)` to assert via the daemon's `pending_params` RPC (`determ pending-params --json`); `--idx` is the entry's 0-based position within its effective-height bucket (the RPC and `build_state_leaves` emit per-height entries in the same order). A NOT-INCLUDED verdict carries `"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"` (F-2 of `docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` — sound only under the (H-neg) honesty premise NV-2/NV-3; NV-6 clause 3: not authoritative absence). Fails closed: INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED → exit 0 (NOT-INCLUDED is a daemon-asserted negative from a daemon `not_found` — (H-neg)), UNVERIFIABLE → exit 3 (legacy daemon that cannot serve `p:`, or any tamper/key-or-value mismatch — never a false INCLUDED), errors → 1. Input is validated before any verdict: `--idx` must fit u32; `--value-hex` must be valid hex (empty allowed — a zero-length param value is legal). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_param_change.sh` (cluster-bound, single-node; SKIP-clean headline INCLUDED when a change is staged, plus always-run random-slot → NOT-INCLUDED, wrong-genesis, out-of-range-`--idx`, and missing-flag rejection assertions). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. **Exit codes**: 0 INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED, 3 UNVERIFIABLE, 1 genesis mismatch / out-of-range or missing args / unreachable daemon. |
| `determ-light verify-param-value --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --name <NAME> --value <U64> [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless **activated-governance-parameter value** verifier — a MATCH / MISMATCH / UNVERIFIABLE verdict on whether the CURRENT effective value of the governance-activated consensus scalar `NAME` equals `U64`, Merkle-anchored to the committee-verified `state_root`. The **activated counterpart** to `verify-param-change`: that command proves a change is still STAGED in `p:` (pending_param_changes); `verify-param-value` proves the value that is LIVE RIGHT NOW in the `k:` (genesis-pinned constants) namespace AFTER `Chain::activate_pending_params` has drained the matured `p:` bucket into the chain-instance scalar and `build_state_leaves` re-committed it under `k:` — the natural query once the chain has advanced past `effective_height` (where `verify-param-change` flips to NOT-INCLUDED). `NAME` is the `build_state_leaves` constant name (lowercase: `min_stake`, `suspension_slash`, `unstake_delay`, `block_subsidy`, `merge_threshold_blocks`, …), NOT the uppercase `PARAM_CHANGE` whitelist token (`activate_pending_params` writes `MIN_STAKE` → `min_stake_`, committed as `"k:min_stake"`). Like `d:`, `k:` is a **simple-key** namespace (`src/node/node.cpp` rpc_state_proof prepends `"k:"` to the raw name — no hex-encoded composite key body), so `--name` rides through verbatim; a `:`-bearing name is rejected as a usage error (counters live under the dedicated `c` namespace). Anchors genesis (fail-closed on hash mismatch), committee-verifies the chain to head, computes the canonical key (`"k:" + name`), fetches the `k:` state-proof, re-anchors `proof.state_root` to a committee-signed header if the chain advanced mid-round-trip (prev_hash walk + sig re-check, identical to `verify-account`), and Merkle-verifies it against the committee-signed `state_root` — gating on `key_bytes == local key` AND comparing `value_hash` to the locally-recomputed `SHA256(u64_be(value))` (matching `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves` `const_leaf`; `append(uint64_t)` is big-endian). **Verdict discipline (distinct from the i:/m:/p: membership readers — every well-known `k:` scalar ALWAYS has a leaf, so a value query is never a membership query):** the leaf Merkle-verifies AND its value_hash matches → **MATCH** (the asserted value IS the live consensus scalar at the anchored head); the leaf Merkle-verifies but its value_hash does NOT match → **MISMATCH** (a SOUND verified negative — the asserted value is provably NOT the current effective value, since the committed leaf itself verified against the committee-signed root); any tamper, `key_bytes` mismatch, malformed proof, stale state, daemon refusal, or `not_found` for an unknown / non-`k:` name → **UNVERIFIABLE** (fail-closed, never a false MATCH). On MISMATCH the verifier deliberately does NOT echo an unverified daemon claim of the live value (`SHA256(u64_be(v))` is non-invertible — a caller recovers the true value by re-running with candidate `--value`s until MATCH, or reads the untrusted hint from `determ pending-params`). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_param_value.sh` (cluster-bound, single-node; asserts a DETERMINISTIC real MATCH against the genesis-pinned `block_subsidy=10` — `k:` constants are committed on every state_root chain, no governance flow required — plus wrong-value → MISMATCH, unknown-name → UNVERIFIABLE/exit3, wrong-genesis fail-closed, `:`-bearing-name + missing-flag usage errors, and anti-false-positive checks). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. **Exit codes**: 0 MATCH/MISMATCH (sound verified answer), 3 UNVERIFIABLE (refused to assert), 1 usage error (`:`-bearing or missing flags) / genesis mismatch / unreachable daemon. |
| `determ-light verify-dapp-registration --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless **DApp-registry membership** verifier (v2.18 Theme 7) — an INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED / UNVERIFIABLE verdict on whether domain `D` is CURRENTLY a registered DApp, i.e. a member of the committee-verified `d:` (dapp_registry) namespace. The `d:`-namespace sibling of the `a:`/`s:` single-leaf reads and the `i:`/`m:`/`p:` composite-key inclusion proofs, completing the trustless-read family across every queryable namespace. Unlike the composite-key readers, `d:` is a **simple-key** namespace (`src/node/node.cpp` rpc_state_proof prepends `"d:"` to the raw domain bytes, like `a:`/`s:`/`r:`), so `--domain` is passed through verbatim (no hex-encoded key body). Anchors genesis, committee-verifies the chain to head, computes the canonical key (`"d:" + domain`), fetches the `d:` state-proof, and Merkle-verifies it against the committee-signed `state_root` — binding the proof to *this* registration via `key_bytes == local key` AND `value_hash == SHA256(service_pubkey[32] ‖ u64_be(registered_at) ‖ u64_be(active_from) ‖ u64_be(inactive_from) ‖ u64_be(url_len) ‖ url ‖ u64_be(topic_count) ‖ for each: u64_be(topic_len) ‖ topic ‖ u64_be(retention) ‖ u64_be(meta_len) ‖ meta)` (matching `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves` `"d:"` branch; metadata bytes appended only when non-empty). **The value_hash binding is load-bearing**: the daemon's `dapp_info` cleartext (service_pubkey, endpoint_url, topics, retention, metadata + the registered_at/active_from/inactive_from heights) is re-hashed locally and must equal the proof's value_hash, so a daemon lie about ANY registration field is detected, not propagated. On INCLUDED the verdict also reports **ACTIVE vs INACTIVE** derived from the committee-attested `inactive_from` vs the anchored head height (a deactivated DApp keeps its `d:` leaf — op=1 sets `inactive_from = height + DAPP_GRACE_BLOCKS` — so INACTIVE is a verified verdict, not a daemon claim; DAPP_CALL is rejected once `inactive_from <= height`). **dapp_registry is mutable**: INCLUDED means "registered AS OF the committee-verified head" (reported with the head height it was proven at). Fails closed: INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED → exit 0 (NOT-INCLUDED is a daemon-asserted negative from a daemon `not_found` — no such DApp registered at the head *if the daemon answers absences honestly*, (H-neg) per `docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` NV-2/NV-3; tagged `"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"` in `--json`, F-2), UNVERIFIABLE → exit 3 (legacy daemon that cannot serve `d:`, an inconsistent daemon whose `dapp_info` disagrees with the committed leaf, or any tamper/key-or-value mismatch — never a false INCLUDED), errors → 1. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_dapp_registration.sh` (cluster-bound, single-node; stands up a real DAPP_REGISTER and asserts a genuine Merkle-verified INCLUDED+ACTIVE, plus unregistered-domain → NOT-INCLUDED, wrong-genesis fail-closed, and missing-flag rejection). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. **Exit codes**: 0 INCLUDED/NOT-INCLUDED, 3 UNVERIFIABLE, 1 genesis mismatch / missing args / unreachable daemon. |
| `determ-light verify-registrant --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --domain <D> [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Trustless **validator-registration membership** verifier — an INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED / UNVERIFIABLE verdict on whether domain `D` is a registered validator (a member of the committee-verified `r:` (registrants) namespace) at the head. **Completes the trustless-read family across all ten S-033 namespaces** (`r:` was the last simple-key namespace without a reader, even though registrants ARE the set the committee is drawn from). The `r:`-namespace sibling of `stake-trustless` (`s:`) and `verify-dapp-registration` (`d:`): anchors genesis, committee-verifies the chain to head, computes the canonical key (`"r:" + domain`), fetches the `r:` state-proof, Merkle-verifies it against the committee-signed `state_root`, and binds the proof to *this* registration via `key_bytes == local key` AND `value_hash == SHA256(ed_pub[32] ‖ u64_be(registered_at) ‖ u64_be(active_from) ‖ u64_be(inactive_from) ‖ u64_be(region_len) ‖ region)` (matching `chain.cpp::build_state_leaves` `"r:"` branch, lines 299-307). **The value_hash binding is load-bearing**: the daemon's `account` RPC `registry` cleartext (`ed_pub`, `registered_at`, `active_from`, `inactive_from`, `region` — the `region` field added for this reader) is re-hashed locally and must equal the proof's value_hash, so a daemon lie about ANY registrant field is detected, not propagated. On INCLUDED the verdict reports **ACTIVE vs INACTIVE** derived from the committee-attested `active_from`/`inactive_from` vs the anchored head (a deregistered validator keeps its `r:` leaf with `inactive_from` set, so INACTIVE is a verified verdict; genesis creators carry `inactive_from = UINT64_MAX` → ACTIVE). A null `registry` with a present `r:` proof is an inconsistent daemon → fail closed; symmetrically, a `not_found` with a NON-null `registry` is also inconsistent → UNVERIFIABLE (this self-consistency cross-check catches a self-contradicting daemon only — a consistent liar still forges the negative, so NOT-INCLUDED stays a **daemon-asserted negative**, (H-neg) per `docs/proofs/NegativeVerdictSoundness.md` NV-2/NV-3, tagged `"negative_footing": "daemon_asserted"` in `--json`, F-2). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_registrant.sh` (offline arg/exit-code contract + cluster-bound live INCLUDED — the genesis creators auto-register into `r:` at block 0, so a node's own domain stands up a real Merkle-verified INCLUDED with no extra tx). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless`. **Exit codes**: 0 INCLUDED / NOT-INCLUDED (daemon-asserted `not_found` negative, (H-neg)), 3 UNVERIFIABLE (tamper / value_hash mismatch / inconsistent daemon — never a false INCLUDED), 1 genesis mismatch / missing args / unreachable daemon. |
| `determ-light verify-state-root --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --height <H> [--json] [--wait <seconds>]` | Per-height committee-verified `state_root` primitive (F3 R40) — reports the **committee-verified `state_root` at a single height `H`**, bound to the operator's pinned genesis, or fail-closed exits. Distinct from `verify-state-proof` (which verifies a Merkle inclusion path against a root the operator already holds): `verify-state-root` is the upstream primitive that *establishes* that trusted root. Anchors genesis ONCE (fail-closed on hash mismatch — "GENESIS HASH MISMATCH"), fetches `header[H]`, walks + verifies the prev_hash chain genesis → H (so `H` is bound to block 0, not a floating header), verifies header[H]'s K-of-K (MD) / `ceil(2K/3)`-of-`k_bft` (BFT) committee Ed25519 sigs, and emits the committee-verified `header[H].state_root`. **Binding mechanism (load-bearing):** `state_root` is NOT directly in the committee-signed `compute_block_digest`; it is bound into `Block::signing_bytes` / `block_hash` (when non-zero) and committee-certified **transitively forward** via `block_hash(H) = prev_hash(H+1) ∈ digest(H+1)` — so the reported root is committee-signed (not daemon-asserted), with the head-block boundary noted (the head's root has no signed successor yet; full nodes enforce it via the apply-layer S-033 gate meanwhile). The standalone form of the anchor `read_account_trustless` performs inline; feed its output to `verify-state-proof --state-root <R>`. On a chain where S-033 is not active (every header's `state_root` is empty) it reports the absence rather than a meaningless zero root, mirroring the in-tree `"chain has not activated state_root (S-033)"` discipline. Soundness proof: `docs/proofs/StateRootAnchorSoundness.md` (SR-1 committee-anchored root via the transitive-forward digest link, SR-2 genesis-binding, SR-3 height-binding, SR-4 fail-closed, SR-5 pre-S-033 vacuity). Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_state_root.sh` (7 assertions — cluster-bound; wrong-genesis fail, tampered-`state_root`-at-`H`-with-valid-digest-sigs fail via the `H+1` link, pre-S-033 reports "S-033 not active"). Supports the opt-in `--wait <seconds>` head-read hold-and-wait, as on `balance-trustless` (the head's `state_root` has no committee-signed successor yet — `--wait` blocks for the next block then binds the already-held proof). **Exit codes**: 0 root emitted (committee-verified), 1 genesis pin mismatch / committee-sig failure / chain break / unreachable daemon / S-033-not-active / args error. |
| `determ-light export-state-bundle --rpc-port <N> --genesis <file> --namespace <ns> --key <K> --out <file>` | **ONLINE producer** (needs a daemon) of an OFFLINE state-proof bundle (commit `8904d33`) — the state-side analog of `export-headers`/`verify-archive`. Captures "key `K` in namespace `NS` had value `V` at anchor height `H`" as a self-contained artifact a third party re-verifies with `verify-state-bundle` and NO daemon. Anchors genesis (fail-closed if the daemon's block 0 doesn't hash to OUR `--genesis`), fetches the `state_proof` for `(NS, K)`, the FULL anchor block at `proof_height-1` (the `block` RPC — needed so `block_hash` is recomputable offline; the stripped `headers` RPC cannot), and the committee-signed SUCCESSOR header at `proof_height`, then **re-verifies the committee→`state_root` binding via the in-tree `committee_bound_state_root` BEFORE writing** (reuses the same online helper as the trustless readers, so the export side never duplicates the binding logic) — only a sound bundle is ever produced. For `ns=="a"` it also stores the account cleartext `{balance, next_nonce}` so the verifier can recompute + match `value_hash`. Refuses to bundle the chain HEAD (no committee-signed successor yet — retry once the chain advances one block) and refuses a wrong-chain daemon or a zero/unpopulated (pre-S-033) anchor `state_root`. Writes a bundle JSON (schema `determ-light-state-bundle/1`: `{schema, genesis_hash, namespace, key, anchor_index, anchor_block, successor_header, state_proof[, account_cleartext]}`). `NS` is one of `a`/`s`/`r`/`d`/`b`/`k`/`c`/`i`/`m`/`p` (composite `i`/`m`/`p` keys hex-encode the binary body). Soundness: `docs/proofs/OfflineStateBundleSoundness.md` (FB63).
