Exercised by `tools/test_light_state_bundle.sh` (cluster/CI round-trip leg). **Exit codes**: 0 bundle written (committee-bound), 1 args / RPC / genesis-mismatch / head-not-bundleable / binding-mismatch / write error. |
| `determ-light verify-state-bundle --in <bundle> --genesis <file> [--json]` | **OFFLINE** verifier of an `export-state-bundle` artifact (commit `8904d33`) — opens NO `RpcClient`, touches NO network; the operator's `--genesis` is the SOLE trust anchor (the committee is derived from it, NOT from a bundle field). Reproduces `committee_bound_state_root` reading from the bundle bytes, gated in order: (1b) **KEY-BINDING** — reconstruct the canonical `key_bytes` from the displayed `(ns,key)` byte-identically to the daemon's `rpc_state_proof` encoding (`src/node/node.cpp:3389-3432`) and require it `== state_proof.key_bytes` (runs FIRST, fail-fast — binds the displayed key to the proven leaf so an honest bundle for `bob` re-labelled `alice` is REFUSED); (2) chain-identity pin `compute_genesis_hash(--genesis) == bundle.genesis_hash`; (3) genesis-seeded committee; (4) recompute `compute_hash(FULL anchor block)`; (5) `verify_block_sigs(successor)` MD + BFT; (6) **THE binding** `successor.prev_hash == recomputed anchor block_hash` (the S-042 binding — `state_root` is committee-bound via `signing_bytes`→`block_hash`, NOT the committee digest); (7) `anchor.state_root == proof.state_root` (non-zero); (8) Merkle-verify the proof against the BOUND root (not the proof's self-claimed root); (9) `ns=="a"`: recompute `value_hash = SHA256(u64_be(balance) ‖ u64_be(next_nonce))` and match. A VERIFIED verdict reports the `(ns,key,value)` at `anchor_index` as committee-attested. Soundness: `docs/proofs/OfflineStateBundleSoundness.md` (FB63 — OSB-MAIN under {A1, A2}; OSB-1 key-binding = the state-side `verify-chain-file` VCF-S analog). Exercised by `tools/test_light_state_bundle.sh` (offline help/missing-`--in`/garbage/wrong-schema/key-binding legs always run; positive round-trip + tamper-`anchor.state_root` / tamper-`successor.prev_hash` / wrong-`--genesis` negatives on the CI/cluster leg). **Exit codes**: 0 VERIFIED, 3 UNVERIFIABLE (any tamper / malformed / sig-fail / binding-fail / key-binding mismatch), 1 args / IO error. |
| `determ-light verify-equivocation --in <event.json> {--pubkey <64-hex> \| --committee <file>} [--json]` | **OFFLINE** equivocation-evidence verifier (FA6) — a per-invocation EQUIVOCATION-PROVEN / NOT-EQUIVOCATION verdict on whether a circulating `EquivocationEvent` (the double-sign proof carried by the `EQUIVOCATION_EVIDENCE` gossip message + the `submit_equivocation` RPC) actually proves a slashable double-sign, without running a full node. Opens NO RPC client and touches NO network — pure local cryptographic re-check. Re-runs the daemon's V11 slash gate (`src/node/validator.cpp::check_equivocation_events`) INDEPENDENTLY: parses the event via the canonical `EquivocationEvent::from_json` (which enforces the field-name + hex-length contract — `digest_a`/`digest_b` 64-hex, `sig_a`/`sig_b` 128-hex), resolves the equivocator's registered Ed25519 key from a source the verifier trusts (`--pubkey` takes the bare 64-hex key; `--committee` resolves it from a `{domain, ed_pub}[]` committee/genesis-committee file by the event's own `equivocator` domain — the key MUST come from a trusted source, never the event itself), then gates on all four V11 conditions: `digest_a != digest_b` (two DISTINCT signed values, not a replay), `sig_a != sig_b` (two distinct signatures), and BOTH `Verify(pk, digest, sig)` succeed against the same registered key. All four holding is cryptographic proof the signer double-signed at one `block_index` (V11 is digest-agnostic — the two hashes may be `block_digest`s OR contrib commitments per the S-006 ContribMsg path): **EQUIVOCATION-PROVEN**, a slash is justified. Any condition failing (equal digests, equal sigs, or a sig that does not verify) is **NOT-EQUIVOCATION**: the evidence does NOT prove a double-sign — fail-closed, never a false PROVEN. Per `docs/proofs/EquivocationSlashing.md` (FA6, T-6) this verdict has **no false positives** under Ed25519 EUF-CMA — an honest validator can never be PROVEN here, since reproducing the event would require forging a signature by an honest key (`<= 2^-128` per attempt). Cross-shard events (`shard_id`/`beacon_anchor_height` nonzero) re-verify by the same two-sig proof (T-6.1) and echo the provenance fields. The trustless read-side counterpart to the daemon's detection + apply path: an auditor, governance script, or counter-party verifies a slash claim BEFORE trusting it. Read the event from stdin with `--in -`. Exercised by `tools/test_light_verify_equivocation.sh` (12 assertions — genuine double-sign → PROVEN, `--committee`-resolved key, wrong key → NOT-EQUIVOCATION, equal-digests/equal-sigs/tampered-sig rejection, unknown-domain & malformed-hex usage errors, stdin path). **Exit codes**: 0 EQUIVOCATION-PROVEN, 3 NOT-EQUIVOCATION (sound refusal to assert a double-sign), 1 malformed event / bad hex / unknown `--committee` domain / missing `--in` / both key sources / args error. |
| `determ-light decode-wire --in <file> [--expect-type <NAME>] [--json]` | OFFLINE decode + structural validation of a single Determ binary wire envelope (A3 / S8 wire-version 1) read from a raw artifact — the message BODY (bytes after the transport-layer `[u32 big-endian length]` frame header). Self-contained: re-implements the published envelope spec in `src/net/binary_codec.cpp` INDEPENDENTLY of the daemon's codec, so it is an external conformance oracle for wire-format drift. Fail-closed checks: 16 MB framing ceiling (`kMaxFrameBytes`); magic `0xB1` + version `0x01` + zero reserved byte; `msg_type` in `[0,18]` (HELLO rejected — it is always JSON pre-negotiation); the S-022 per-type body cap (`max_message_bytes`: 1 MB chatter / 4 MB block-class / 16 MB snapshot+chain); and payload well-formedness — the TRANSACTION 4×256-bit frame + trailer (reserved slot zero, exact lengths, no trailing bytes) or the `[u32 LE json_len][json]` wrapper for every other type (declared length matches the body exactly and parses as JSON). `--expect-type` asserts the decoded MsgType name (case-insensitive). Exercised by `tools/test_light_decode_wire.sh`. **Exit codes**: 0 VALID, 3 MALFORMED (structural spec violation), 1 I/O / usage error. |
| `determ-light shard-route --genesis <file> --address <addr\|domain> [--json]` | **OFFLINE** genesis-pinned address-to-shard routing oracle (R41 sharding) — reports which shard OWNS `<addr>` on the chain pinned by `<genesis>`, opening NO RPC client and touching NO network. Unlike the daemon's `determ where-is` (which takes shard count + salt as raw operator flags), `shard-route` reads BOTH routing parameters FROM the genesis itself (`initial_shard_count` + `shard_address_salt`) — both CSPRNG-fixed at build time and bound into `compute_genesis_hash` (see `include/determ/crypto/random.hpp`), so the home shard of any address is a function of the chain identity alone. Re-implements `crypto::shard_id_for_address` INDEPENDENTLY of the daemon's codec (the light client never links `crypto/random.cpp`): `shard_count <= 1` -> shard 0 (unsharded, no salt mixing); otherwise `h = SHA256(shard_address_salt ‖ "shard-route" ‖ addr)`, `shard = fold_be8(h[0..7]) % shard_count` — byte-for-byte matching `src/crypto/random.cpp`. Anon-form addresses (`0x` + 64 hex) are normalized to canonical lowercase first (S-028), so `0xABC…` and `0xabc…` route identically (matching the chain's pre-routing canonicalization before `is_cross_shard`); domains and other shapes route on their exact bytes (case-sensitive, upstream validation is the caller's responsibility). Prints the locally computed `genesis_hash` so the operator can confirm the routing is anchored to the expected chain — a wrong-genesis file yields a different hash AND, in general, a different home shard. `--json` emits `{address, routed_address, anon, shard, shard_count, genesis_hash}`. Pure local computation — no daemon, no RPC, no UNVERIFIABLE state (the genesis IS the trust anchor, so a parseable genesis always yields a sound deterministic home shard). Exercised by `tools/test_light_shard_route.sh` (offline; cross-checks every probe address against `determ where-is` as an independent conformance oracle, plus unsharded-count=1 → shard 0, anon case normalization, distinct-salt → distinct genesis_hash, missing-`--address` and malformed-salt-S-018 rejection). **Exit codes**: 0 routing emitted, 1 missing `--address` / `--genesis` / genesis parse error (e.g. `shard_address_salt` not 64-hex, S-018). |
| `determ-light rpc-auth --secret <hex> --method <NAME> [--params-file <f> \| --params-string <json> \| --params-stdin] [--expect <hex>] [--emit-request] [--json]` | Offline compute/verify of the S-001 HMAC-SHA256 RPC auth tag (`HMAC(secret, method + "\|" + params.dump())`), independently re-implementing src/rpc/rpc.cpp. Compute prints the tag (or `--emit-request` a full `{method,params,auth}`); `--expect` constant-time verifies → MATCH (0) / MISMATCH (3); usage/bad-hex → 1. No daemon. |
| `determ-light help` / `--help` / `-h` | Print the full subcommand surface + trust-model overview. |
| `determ-light version` / `--version` | Print binary version (currently `determ-light 1.0.0`). |
